- [AVPV/PeN kisspeptin neuron, mouse](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020073) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A hypothalamic kisspeptin neuron with its soma located in the anteroventral periventricular nucleus (AVPV) and the posterior part of the periventricular hypothalamic nucleus in the rostral hypothalamus (Stephens et al., 2017; Nejad et al., 2017). It mediates estrogen positive feedback by driving gonadotropin-releasing hormone (GnRH) and luteinizing hormone (LH) secretion and is required for the preovulatory LH surge (Adachi et al., 2007; Nejad et al., 2017). In mice, it co-expresses kisspeptin (Kiss1) and tyrosine hydroxylase (TH), indicating a dopaminergic component within an otherwise primarily GABAergic phenotype (Kauffman et al., 2007; Stephens et al., 2017, 2024). It also expresses estrogen receptor alpha (Esr1), enabling direct regulation by estradiol (Frazao et al., 2013; Wartenberg et al., 2021). It belongs to a sexually dimorphic population, with higher cell numbers observed in females than in males in rodents (Stephens et al., 2017; Nejad et al., 2017)."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string)

- [CA1 pyramidal cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020072) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A hippocampal pyramidal neuron with soma located in the pyramidal layer of hippocampal area CA1 (Cembrowski et al., 2016; M&uuml;ller &amp; Remy, 2017), forming the dominant excitatory projection population of the CA1 subfield. As the primary output cell of Ammon's horn, it projects via the subiculum to entorhinal cortex and is capable of glutamate secretion as a neurotransmitter (Dale et al., 2015). In mouse, it is distinguished from CA2 and CA3 pyramidal neurons by soma position within the CA1 stratum pyramidale and by expression of wolframin (Wfs1), an endoplasmic reticulum-resident membrane protein enriched in deep-sublayer CA1 cells (Cembrowski et al., 2016)."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string)

- [CA2 pyramidal cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020070) [id](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#id) "CL:0020070"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [CA2 pyramidal cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020070) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A hippocampal pyramidal neuron with soma located in the pyramidal layer of hippocampal area CA2 (Cembrowski et al., 2016; Sanchez-Aguilera et al., 2021). Distinguished from CA1 and CA3 pyramidal neurons by expression of Pcp4, Rgs14, and Amigo2 in rodents (San Antonio et al., 2014; Caruana et al., 2012), and by absence of the CA1 marker wolframin (Wfs1) (Evans et al., 2018). Receives strong LTP-competent input from entorhinal cortex at distal dendrites, while Schaffer collateral inputs to proximal dendrites are resistant to canonical LTP in wild-type animals (Chevaleyre &amp; Siegelbaum, 2010). Required for social memory in mice (Hitti &amp; Siegelbaum, 2014)."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string)

### CA3 pyramidal cell `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020068`

#### Added

- [CA3 pyramidal cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020068) [contributor](http://purl.org/dc/terms/contributor) [0000-0002-5507-2103](https://orcid.org/0000-0002-5507-2103) 

- [CA3 pyramidal cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020068) [date](http://purl.org/dc/terms/date) "2026-05-26T14:55:38Z"^^[dateTime](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#dateTime) 

- [CA3 pyramidal cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020068) [id](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#id) "CL:0020068"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [CA3 pyramidal cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020068) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A hippocampal pyramidal neuron with soma located in the pyramidal layer of hippocampal area CA3 (Cembrowski et al., 2016; Wheeler et al., 2015). Capable of glutamate secretion as a neurotransmitter (Dale et al., 2015) and distinguished from CA1 and CA2 pyramidal neurons by thorny excrescences on the proximal apical dendrites &mdash; postsynaptic specializations that receive excitatory mossy fiber input from dentate gyrus granule cells (Munster-Wandowski et al., 2013). Harbours a dense recurrent Schaffer collateral network; individual neurons can act as hub neurons capable of triggering hippocampal network bursts (Marissal et al., 2012)."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 
  - [database_cross_reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:24319410"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

  - [database_cross_reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:26402459"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

  - [database_cross_reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:27113915"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string)

- [Oriens-Lacunosum Moleculare neuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020074) [date](http://purl.org/dc/terms/date) "2026-04-10T10:48:46Z"^^[dateTime](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#dateTime) 

- [Oriens-Lacunosum Moleculare neuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020074) [id](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#id) "CL:0020074"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [Oriens-Lacunosum Moleculare neuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020074) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A GABAergic interneuron of the hippocampal CA1 region whose horizontally oriented soma is located in the stratum oriens at the stratum oriens&ndash;alveus border, with spiny dendrites confined to stratum oriens; the axon ascends vertically to arborize exclusively in stratum lacunosum-moleculare, innervating the apical tufts of pyramidal neurons. Electrophysiologically, these cells display regular-to-adapting spiking with a prominent hyperpolarization-activated cation current (Ih) and theta-frequency resonance. In rodents, canonical markers include somatostatin (Sst) and metabotropic glutamate receptor 1 (Grm1/mGluR1); the alpha-2 nicotinic acetylcholine receptor subunit (Chrna2) is a highly specific marker in mouse."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string)

  - [database_cross_reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:20421280"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string)

- [entorhinal cortex layer II stellate cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020067) [date](http://purl.org/dc/terms/date) "2026-05-05T13:19:02Z"^^[dateTime](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#dateTime) 

- [entorhinal cortex layer II stellate cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020067) [id](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#id) "CL:0020067"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [entorhinal cortex layer II stellate cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020067) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A glutamatergic principal neuron with its soma located in layer II of the entorhinal cortex, distinguished by stellate morphology, lack of calbindin expression, and expression of reelin in rodents. This cell type is a major source of perforant pathway projections from entorhinal cortex layer II to the dentate gyrus of the hippocampal formation. It displays electrophysiological properties including a prominent hyperpolarisation-activated inward current, voltage sag, and theta-frequency membrane resonance."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string)

- [hilar mossy cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020069) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A dentate gyrus neuron with soma in the polymorphic layer (Scharfman &amp; Myers, 2012), capable of glutamate secretion as a neurotransmitter (Scharfman &amp; Bernstein, 2015). Distinguished by a large multipolar soma, thorny excrescences on proximal dendrites, and commissural/associational axon projections terminating in the inner molecular layer of the dentate gyrus (Scharfman &amp; Myers, 2012). In rodents, serves as a major excitatory neuron of the dentate hilus providing feedback excitation to granule cells (Sun et al., 2017)."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 
  - [database_cross_reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:23420672"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

  - [database_cross_reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:26347618"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

  - [database_cross_reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:33600026"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

  - [database_cross_reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:34214666"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

  - [database_cross_reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:28451637"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string)

### parvalbumin-positive basket cell `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020071`

#### Added
- Class: [parvalbumin-positive basket cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020071) 

- [parvalbumin-positive basket cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020071) [IAO_0000233](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000233) [3644](https://github.com/obophenotype/cell-ontology/issues/3644) 

- [parvalbumin-positive basket cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020071) [contributor](http://purl.org/dc/terms/contributor) [0000-0002-5507-2103](https://orcid.org/0000-0002-5507-2103) 

- [parvalbumin-positive basket cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020071) [date](http://purl.org/dc/terms/date) "2026-05-19T14:15:42Z"^^[dateTime](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#dateTime) 

- [parvalbumin-positive basket cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020071) [id](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#id) "CL:0020071"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [parvalbumin-positive basket cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020071) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A basket cell of the hippocampal formation that expresses the calcium-binding protein parvalbumin (Pvalb) in rodents (Rivera et al., 2014; Que et al., 2021; Contreras et al., 2019). Somata are located in the pyramidal layers of CA1 and CA3 and the granule cell layer of the dentate gyrus. Axon collaterals are confined to the pyramidal layer, forming dense perisomatic inhibitory synapses on the somata of principal neurons; a single cell contacts more than 1500 pyramidal neurons (Sik et al., 1995). This cell is a fast-spiking GABAergic interneuron and is distinguished from CCK basket cells by absence of cannabinoid receptor 1 (Cnr1) expression (Whissell et al., 2015)."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 
  - [database_cross_reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:7472426"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

  - [database_cross_reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:25018703"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

  - [database_cross_reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:33398060"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

  - [database_cross_reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:31297048"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

  - [database_cross_reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:26441554"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string)
